[30;1m78 | [0m[35mOnce you've marked code for deprecation via :func:`~deprecation.deprecated`,[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35myou can sit back and relax as most of the work has been done for you.[0m
[30;1m80 | [0m[35mAssuming you've provided sufficient detail to the decorator, you now just[0m
[30;1m81 | [0m[35mwait for your tests to tell you it's time to delete the code in question.[0m
[30;1m82 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m83 | [0m[35mIf you wrap test methods which use your now deprecated code in[0m
[30;1m84 | [0m[35m:func:`~deprecation.fail_if_not_removed`, the test will fail with a message[0m
